true)(set: $visitjapanese to false) } (align:"<==")+(box:"====XXXXX=")[''INTRODUCTION''] The year is 2054 and finally the fallout from the nuclear war has receded in some areas, making them barely habitable again. This war began between the union of globalist governments, known as the Empire, and countries who wanted to live independantly, almost resulting in the end of civilization. The human species however proved durable enough - although many have died, there are survivors agianst all odds. Even more - certain technologies developed before the war also survived and thrived in this new world, exceeding all expectations. The most notable of them is the waifu - a beautiful and obedient sex robot, pleasing its master and also giving birth to his children. Despite the destruction of the old world companies like The Doll Warehouse have rebuilt and developed that technology into a thriving business, selling waifus across the wasteland. One of the reasons why waifus have mostly replaced biological women is that before the war women were under the delusion that they don't need men and so they drifted apart. Because of that when the bombs fell, most women simply couldn't survive on their own and died, except for the more young and beautiful ones who managed to find a men when their need was dire. This is the world you live in - a wasteland populated by scavanging bandits, dangerous beasts and many secrets waiting to be uncovered. Also if you have the silver, you can get yourself some nice company. Few notes before you start: ''1. Saving/Loading the game'' - You have a SAVE button in the Bunker, which is your base and main page. You can then click LOAD GAME in the starter page and you will continue where you left off. ''PLEASE NOTE ''- ''the saves are kept only in your browser, so if you delete cookies and history your save will be lost.'' ''2. Fighting'' - in combat you have four things to track - your warband health, your warband damage, your enemies health and enemies damage. When you click Fight a calculation happens where damage from one party is deducted once from the health of the other party. Whoever health reaches 0 loses and the other wins, it's that simple. If the health of both sides reaches 0, you still lose. In every fight you have the option to run away which spends all your energy and halves your personal health (not the total warband health). ''PLEASE NOTE - if your warband health is under 70 you will die if you try to run''. You have to calculate before pressing that Fight button. There are many factors which contribute to your warband health and damage - the weapons you use, the number of warriors from your waifus offspring and others. ''3. Waifus'' - waifus are beautiful and obedient sex robots, ready to please you and give birth to your children. The pregnancy of a waifu is short - only 30 days and after that the offspring grows into adult in matter of hours, with biologically embedded skills and loyalty to their father. Because of their DNA matrix there are 3 main types of offspring - farmer, scavanger and warrior. ''They all consume 1 food per day.'' ''The farmer feeds himsef and produces aditional 2 food. The scavanger increases the resources you find. The warrior adds 25 damage and 100 health to your warband strenght. '' Your waifus are located in your Harem where you can see how much is left until birth. You collect your offsrping in the Nursery. ''4. Food'' - you and your farmer offspring produce food in the Garden, make sure you don't go negative or you will die! ''5. Places to go'' - when you leave your Bunker and go Outside there are places you can visit to trade or collect resources. More places can be uncovered as you explore the wasteland. //*If people show interest I may add more to the game, but keep in mind that I am not a pro developer and I work only with Twine Harlow.
